4633 
4634 /* Definitions used in the body of the `gconv' function.  */
4635 #define CHARSET_NAME        "EUC-JP-MS//"
4636 #define FROM_LOOP       from_eucjp_ms
4637 #define TO_LOOP         to_eucjp_ms
4638 #define DEFINE_INIT     1
4639 #define DEFINE_FINI     1
4640 #define MIN_NEEDED_FROM     1
4641 #define MAX_NEEDED_FROM     3
4642 #define MIN_NEEDED_TO       4
4643 #define ONE_DIRECTION       0
4644 
4645 
4646 /* First define the conversion function from EUC-JP-MS to UCS4.  */
4647 #define MIN_NEEDED_INPUT    MIN_NEEDED_FROM
4648 #define MAX_NEEDED_INPUT    MAX_NEEDED_FROM
4649 #define MIN_NEEDED_OUTPUT   MIN_NEEDED_TO
4650 #define LOOPFCT         FROM_LOOP
4651 #define BODY \
4652   {                                       \
4653     uint32_t ch = (uint32_t)inptr[0] & 0xff;                      \
4654                                           \
4655     if (ch < 0x8e || (ch >= 0x90 && ch <= 0x9f))                  \
4656       ++inptr;                                    \
4657     else if (ch == 0xff)                              \
4658       {                                       \
4659     /* This is illegal.  */                           \
4660     if (! ignore_errors_p ())                         \
4661       {                                   \
4662         result = __GCONV_ILLEGAL_INPUT;                   \
4663         break;                                \
4664       }                                   \
4665                                           \
4666     ++inptr;                                  \
4667     ++*irreversible;                              \
4668     continue;                                 \
4669       }                                       \
4670     else                                      \
4671       {                                       \
4672     /* Two or more byte character.  First test whether the next       \
4673        character is also available.  */                   \
4674     unsigned char ch2;                            \
4675                                           \
4676     if (__glibc_unlikely (inptr + 1 >= inend))                \
4677       {                                   \
4678         /* The second character is not available.  Store the          \
4679            intermediate result.  */                       \
4680         result = __GCONV_INCOMPLETE_INPUT;                    \
4681         break;                                \
4682       }                                   \
4683                                           \
4684     ch2 = (unsigned char)inptr[1];                        \
4685                                           \
4686     /* All second bytes of a multibyte character must be >= 0xa1. */      \
4687     if (__glibc_unlikely (ch2 < 0xa1))                    \
4688       {                                   \
4689         /* This is an illegal character.  */                  \
4690         if (! ignore_errors_p ())                         \
4691           {                                   \
4692         result = __GCONV_ILLEGAL_INPUT;                   \
4693         break;                                \
4694           }                                   \
4695                                           \
4696         ++inptr;                                  \
4697         ++*irreversible;                              \
4698         continue;                                 \
4699       }                                   \
4700                                           \
4701     if (__builtin_expect(ch == 0x8e, 0))                      \
4702       {                                   \
4703         /* This is code set 2: half-width katakana.  */           \
4704         ch = jisx0201_to_ucs4 (ch2);                      \
4705         /*if (__builtin_expect (ch, 0) == __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR)*/         \
4706         if (__glibc_unlikely (ch == __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR))            \
4707           {                                   \
4708         /* Illegal character.  */                     \
4709         if (! ignore_errors_p ())                     \
4710           {                               \
4711             /* This is an illegal character.  */              \
4712             result = __GCONV_ILLEGAL_INPUT;               \
4713             break;                            \
4714           }                               \
4715           }                                   \
4716                                           \
4717         inptr += 2;                               \
4718       }                                   \
4719     else                                      \
4720       {                                   \
4721         const unsigned char *endp = inptr;                    \
4722         int mblen = 1;                            \
4723                                           \
4724         if (__builtin_expect(ch == 0x8f, 0))                  \
4725           {                                   \
4726         if (inend - inptr < 3)                        \
4727           ch = 0;                             \
4728         else                                  \
4729           {                               \
4730             unsigned char ch3 = (unsigned char)inptr[2];          \
4731             mblen = 3;                            \
4732                                           \
4733             if (__builtin_expect(ch3 == 0xff, 0)              \
4734                 || __builtin_expect(ch3 < 0xa1, 0))           \
4735               ch = __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR;                  \
4736             else if (ch2 <= 0xf2)                     \
4737               {                               \
4738                 endp = inptr + 1;                     \
4739                                           \
4740                 /* This is code set 3: JIS X 0212-1990.  */       \
4741                 ch = jisx0212_to_ucs4 (&endp, inend - endp, 0x80);    \
4742                                           \
4743                 if (ch == 0x00a6) /* BROKEN BAR */            \
4744                   ch = 0xffe4;    /* FULLWIDTH BROKEN BAR */          \
4745                 else if (ch == __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR)              \
4746                   endp -= 1;                          \
4747               }                               \
4748             else if (ch2 <= 0xf4)                     \
4749               {                               \
4750                 int idx = ((ch2-0xf3)*94 + ch3-0xa1) - (94-12);       \
4751                                           \
4752                 if (0 <= idx && idx < 12 + 94)                \
4753                   {                           \
4754                 if ((ch = cjk_block_ibm[idx]) != 0)           \
4755                   endp = inptr + mblen;               \
4756                 else                          \
4757                       ch = __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR;              \
4758                   }                           \
4759                 else                              \
4760               ch = __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR;                  \
4761               }                               \
4762             else if (ch2 <= 0xfe)                     \
4763               {                               \
4764                 ch = 0xe3ac + (ch2 - 0xf5) * 94 + (ch3 - 0xa1);       \
4765                 endp = inptr + mblen;                     \
4766               }                               \
4767             else                              \
4768               ch = __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR;                  \
4769           }                               \
4770           }                                   \
4771         else if (__builtin_expect(0xa1 <= ch, 1))                 \
4772           {                                   \
4773         mblen = 2;                            \
4774                                           \
4775         if (inend - inptr < 2)                        \
4776           ch = 0;                             \
4777         else if (__builtin_expect(ch2 == 0xff, 0))            \
4778           ch = __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR;                      \
4779         else if (ch <= 0xa8)                          \
4780           {                               \
4781             if ((ch = cjk_block1[(ch-0xa1)*94 + (ch2-0xa1)]) != 0)    \
4782               endp = inptr + mblen;                   \
4783             else                              \
4784               ch = __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR;                  \
4785           }                               \
4786         else if (ch == 0xad)                          \
4787           {                               \
4788             if ((ch = cjk_block2[(ch-0xad)*94 + (ch2-0xa1)]) != 0)    \
4789               endp = inptr + mblen;                   \
4790             else                              \
4791               ch = __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR;                  \
4792           }                               \
4793         else if (ch <= 0xf4)                          \
4794           {                               \
4795             endp = inptr;                         \
4796                                           \
4797             /* This is code set 1: JIS X 0208.  */            \
4798             ch = jisx0208_to_ucs4 (&endp, inend - inptr, 0x80);       \
4799           }                               \
4800         else if (ch <= 0xfe)                          \
4801           {                               \
4802             ch = 0xe000 + (ch - 0xf5) * 94 + (ch2 - 0xa1);        \
4803             endp = inptr + mblen;                     \
4804           }                               \
4805             else                                  \
4806           ch = __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR;                      \
4807           }                                   \
4808         else                                  \
4809           ch = __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR;                      \
4810                                           \
4811         if (__builtin_expect (ch, 1) == 0)                    \
4812           {                                   \
4813         /* Not enough input available.  */                \
4814         result = __GCONV_INCOMPLETE_INPUT;                \
4815         break;                                \
4816           }                                   \
4817         if (__builtin_expect (ch, 0) == __UNKNOWN_10646_CHAR)         \
4818           {                                   \
4819         /* Illegal character.  */                     \
4820         if (! ignore_errors_p ())                     \
4821           {                               \
4822             /* This is an illegal character.  */              \
4823             result = __GCONV_ILLEGAL_INPUT;               \
4824             break;                            \
4825           }                               \
4826                                           \
4827         inptr += mblen;                           \
4828         ++*irreversible;                          \
4829         continue;                             \
4830           }                                   \
4831         inptr = endp;                             \
4832       }                                   \
4833       }                                       \
4834                                           \
4835     put32 (outptr, ch);                               \
4836     outptr += 4;                                  \
4837   }
4838 #define LOOP_NEED_FLAGS
4839 #include <iconv/loop.c>
4840 
4841 
4842 /* Next, define the other direction.  */
4843 #define MIN_NEEDED_INPUT    MIN_NEEDED_TO
4844 #define MIN_NEEDED_OUTPUT   MIN_NEEDED_FROM
4845 #define MAX_NEEDED_OUTPUT   MAX_NEEDED_FROM
4846 #define LOOPFCT         TO_LOOP
4847 #define BODY \
4848   {                                       \
4849     uint32_t ch = get32 (inptr);                          \
4850     const unsigned char *cp;                              \
4851     unsigned char pua[2];                             \
4852                                           \
4853     if (ch >= (sizeof (from_ucs4_lat1) / sizeof (from_ucs4_lat1[0])))         \
4854       {                                       \
4855     if (ch >= 0x0100 && ch <= 0x045f)                     \
4856       cp = from_ucs4_greek[ch - 0x0100];                      \
4857     else if (ch >= 0x2010 && ch <= 0x9fa5)                    \
4858       cp = from_ucs4_cjk[ch - 0x2010];                    \
4859     else if (ch >= 0xe000 && ch <= 0xe757)                    \
4860           {                                   \
4861         if (ch < 0xe3ac)                              \
4862           {                                   \
4863         pua[0] = (ch - 0xe000) / 94 + 0xf5;               \
4864         pua[1] = (ch - 0xe000) % 94 + 0xa1;               \
4865           }                                   \
4866         else                                  \
4867           {                                   \
4868         pua[0] = (ch - 0xe3ac) / 94 + 0xf5;               \
4869         pua[1] = (ch - 0xe3ac) % 94 + 0x21;               \
4870           }                                   \
4871         cp = (const unsigned char *)&pua[0];                  \
4872       }                                   \
4873     else if (ch >= 0xf929 && ch <= 0xfa2d)                    \
4874       cp = from_ucs4_cjkcpt[ch - 0xf929];                     \
4875     else if (__builtin_expect (ch >= 0xff01, 1)               \
4876          && __builtin_expect (ch <= 0xffe5, 1))               \
4877       cp = from_ucs4_extra[ch - 0xff01];                      \
4878     else                                      \
4879       {                                   \
4880         UNICODE_TAG_HANDLER (ch, 4);                      \
4881         /* Illegal character.  */                         \
4882         cp = (const unsigned char *) "";                      \
4883       }                                   \
4884       }                                       \
4885     else                                      \
4886       cp = from_ucs4_lat1[ch];                            \
4887                                           \
4888     if (__builtin_expect (cp[0], '\1') == '\0' && ch != 0)            \
4889       {                                       \
4890     /* Illegal character.  */                         \
4891     STANDARD_TO_LOOP_ERR_HANDLER (4);                     \
4892       }                                       \
4893     else                                      \
4894       {                                       \
4895     *outptr = cp[0];                              \
4896     /* Now test for a possible second byte and write this if possible.  */\
4897     if (cp[1] != '\0')                            \
4898       {                                   \
4899         if (__glibc_unlikely (outptr + 1 >= outend))              \
4900           {                                   \
4901         /* The result does not fit into the buffer.  */           \
4902         result = __GCONV_FULL_OUTPUT;                     \
4903         break;                                \
4904           }                                   \
4905         if (__glibc_unlikely (cp[1] < 0x80))                  \
4906           {                                   \
4907         if (__glibc_unlikely (outptr + 2 >= outend))              \
4908           {                               \
4909             /* The result does not fit into the buffer.  */       \
4910             result = __GCONV_FULL_OUTPUT;                 \
4911             break;                            \
4912           }                               \
4913         *outptr = 0x8f;                           \
4914         *++outptr = cp[0];                        \
4915         *++outptr = cp[1] | 0x80;                     \
4916           }                                   \
4917         else                                  \
4918           *++outptr = cp[1];                          \
4919       }                                   \
4920     ++outptr;                                 \
4921       }                                       \
4922                                           \
4923     inptr += 4;                                   \
4924   }
4925 #define LOOP_NEED_FLAGS
4926 #include <iconv/loop.c>
4927

4929 /* Now define the toplevel functions.  */
4930 #include <iconv/skeleton.c>
